35 class bitmap_image
36 {
37 public:
38 
39  enum channel_mode {
40  rgb_mode = 0,
41  bgr_mode = 1
42  };
43 
44  enum color_plane {
45  blue_plane = 0,
46  green_plane = 1,
47  red_plane = 2
48  };

50 
51  bitmap_image()
52  : file_name_(""),
53  data_ (0),
54  length_(0),
55  width_ (0),
56  height_(0),
57  row_increment_(0),
58  bytes_per_pixel_(3),
59  channel_mode_(bgr_mode)
60  {}
61 
62  bitmap_image(const std::string& filename)
63  : file_name_(filename),
64  data_ (0),
65  length_(0),
66  width_ (0),
67  height_(0),
68  row_increment_(0),
69  bytes_per_pixel_(0),
70  channel_mode_(bgr_mode)
71  {
72  load_bitmap();
73  }

75  bitmap_image(const unsigned int width, const unsigned int height)
76  : file_name_(""),
77  data_ (0),
78  length_(0),
79  width_(width),
80  height_(height),
81  row_increment_(0),
82  bytes_per_pixel_(3),
83  channel_mode_(bgr_mode)
84  {
85  create_bitmap();

88  bitmap_image(const bitmap_image& image)
89  : file_name_(image.file_name_),
90  data_(0),
91  width_(image.width_),
92  height_(image.height_),
93  row_increment_(0),
94  bytes_per_pixel_(3),
95  channel_mode_(bgr_mode)
96  {
97  create_bitmap();
98  std::copy(image.data_, image.data_ + image.length_, data_);
99  }
100 
101  ~bitmap_image()
102  {
103  delete [] data_;
104  }

106  bitmap_image& operator=(const bitmap_image& image)
107  {
108  if (this != &image)
109  {
110  file_name_ = image.file_name_;
111  bytes_per_pixel_ = image.bytes_per_pixel_;
112  width_ = image.width_;
113  height_ = image.height_;
114  row_increment_ = 0;
115  channel_mode_ = image.channel_mode_;
116  create_bitmap();
117  std::copy(image.data_, image.data_ + image.length_, data_);
118  }
119 
120  return *this;
121  }
122 
123  inline bool operator!()
124  {
125  return (data_ == 0) ||
126  (length_ == 0) ||
127  (width_ == 0) ||
128  (height_ == 0) ||
129  (row_increment_== 0);
130  }

132  inline void clear(const unsigned char v = 0x00)
133  {
134  std::fill(data_,data_ + length_,v);
135  }

137  inline unsigned char red_channel(const unsigned int x, const unsigned int y) const
138  {
139  return data_[(y * row_increment_) + (x * bytes_per_pixel_ + 2)];
140  }
141 
142  inline unsigned char green_channel(const unsigned int x, const unsigned int y) const
143  {
144  return data_[(y * row_increment_) + (x * bytes_per_pixel_ + 1)];
145  }
146 
147  inline unsigned char blue_channel (const unsigned int x, const unsigned int y) const
148  {
149  return data_[(y * row_increment_) + (x * bytes_per_pixel_ + 0)];
150  }
151 
152  inline void red_channel(const unsigned int x, const unsigned int y, const unsigned char value)
153  {
154  data_[(y * row_increment_) + (x * bytes_per_pixel_ + 2)] = value;
155  }
156 
157  inline void green_channel(const unsigned int x, const unsigned int y, const unsigned char value)
158  {
159  data_[(y * row_increment_) + (x * bytes_per_pixel_ + 1)] = value;
160  }
161 
162  inline void blue_channel (const unsigned int x, const unsigned int y, const unsigned char value)
163  {
164  data_[(y * row_increment_) + (x * bytes_per_pixel_ + 0)] = value;
165  }

167  inline unsigned char* row(unsigned int row_index) const
168  {
169  return data_ + (row_index * row_increment_);
170  }

172  inline void get_pixel(const unsigned int x, const unsigned int y,
173  unsigned char& red,
174  unsigned char& green,
175  unsigned char& blue)
176  {
177  const unsigned int y_offset = y * row_increment_;
178  const unsigned int x_offset = x * bytes_per_pixel_;
179  blue = data_[y_offset + x_offset + 0];
180  green = data_[y_offset + x_offset + 1];
181  red = data_[y_offset + x_offset + 2];
182  }
183 
184  inline void set_pixel(const unsigned int x, const unsigned int y,
185  const unsigned char red,
186  const unsigned char green,
187  const unsigned char blue)
188  {
189  const unsigned int y_offset = y * row_increment_;
190  const unsigned int x_offset = x * bytes_per_pixel_;
191  data_[y_offset + x_offset + 0] = blue;
192  data_[y_offset + x_offset + 1] = green;
193  data_[y_offset + x_offset + 2] = red;
194  }

196  inline bool copy_from(const bitmap_image& image)
197  {
198  if (
199  (image.height_ != height_) ||
200  (image.width_ != width_ )
201  )
202  {
203  return false;
204  }
205 
206  std::copy(image.data_,image.data_ + image.length_,data_);
207  return true;
208  }
209 
210  inline bool copy_from(const bitmap_image& source_image,
211  const unsigned int& x_offset,
212  const unsigned int& y_offset)
213  {
214  if ((x_offset + source_image.width_ ) > width_ ) { return false; }
215  if ((y_offset + source_image.height_) > height_) { return false; }
216 
217  for (unsigned int y = 0; y < source_image.height_; ++y)
218  {
219  unsigned char* itr1 = row(y + y_offset) + x_offset * bytes_per_pixel_;
220  const unsigned char* itr2 = source_image.row(y);
221  const unsigned char* itr2_end = itr2 + source_image.width_ * bytes_per_pixel_;
222  std::copy(itr2,itr2_end,itr1);
223  }
224  return true;
225  }
226 
227  inline bool region(const unsigned int& x,
228  const unsigned int& y,
229  const unsigned int& width,
230  const unsigned int& height,
231  bitmap_image& dest_image)
232  {
233  if ((x + width ) > width_ ) { return false; }
234  if ((y + height) > height_) { return false; }
235 
236  if (
237  (dest_image.width_ < width_ ) ||
238  (dest_image.height_ < height_)
239  )
240  {
241  dest_image.setwidth_height(width,height);
242  }
243 
244  for (unsigned int r = 0; r < height; ++r)
245  {
246  unsigned char* itr1 = row(r + y) + x * bytes_per_pixel_;
247  unsigned char* itr1_end = itr1 + (width * bytes_per_pixel_);
248  unsigned char* itr2 = dest_image.row(r);
249  std::copy(itr1,itr1_end,itr2);
250  }
251 
252  return true;
253  }
254 
255  inline bool set_region(const unsigned int& x,
256  const unsigned int& y,
257  const unsigned int& width,
258  const unsigned int& height,
259  const unsigned char& value)
260  {
261  if ((x + width) > width_) { return false; }
262  if ((y + height) > height_) { return false; }
263 
264  for (unsigned int r = 0; r < height; ++r)
265  {
266  unsigned char* itr = row(r + y) + x * bytes_per_pixel_;
267  unsigned char* itr_end = itr + (width * bytes_per_pixel_);
268  std::fill(itr,itr_end,value);
269  }
270 
271  return true;
272  }
273 
274  inline bool set_region(const unsigned int& x,
275  const unsigned int& y,
276  const unsigned int& width,
277  const unsigned int& height,
278  const color_plane color,
279  const unsigned char& value)
280  {
281  if ((x + width) > width_) { return false; }
282  if ((y + height) > height_) { return false; }
283 
284  const unsigned int color_plane_offset = offset(color);
285 
286  for (unsigned int r = 0; r < height; ++r)
287  {
288  unsigned char* itr = row(r + y) + x * bytes_per_pixel_ + color_plane_offset;
289  unsigned char* itr_end = itr + (width * bytes_per_pixel_);
290 
291  while (itr != itr_end)
292  {
293  *itr = value;
294  itr += bytes_per_pixel_;
295  }
296  }
297 
298  return true;
299  }
300 
301  inline bool set_region(const unsigned int& x,
302  const unsigned int& y,
303  const unsigned int& width,
304  const unsigned int& height,
305  const unsigned char& red,
306  const unsigned char& green,
307  const unsigned char& blue)
308  {
309  if ((x + width) > width_) { return false; }
310  if ((y + height) > height_) { return false; }
311 
312  for (unsigned int r = 0; r < height; ++r)
313  {
314  unsigned char* itr = row(r + y) + x * bytes_per_pixel_;
315  unsigned char* itr_end = itr + (width * bytes_per_pixel_);
316 
317  while (itr != itr_end)
318  {
319  *(itr++) = blue;
320  *(itr++) = green;
321  *(itr++) = red;
322  }
323  }
324 
325  return true;
326  }
327 
328  void reflective_image(bitmap_image& image)
329  {
330  image.setwidth_height(3 * width_, 3 * height_,true);
331  image.copy_from(*this,width_,height_);
332  vertical_flip();
333  image.copy_from(*this,width_,0);
334  image.copy_from(*this,width_,2 * height_);
335  vertical_flip();
336  horizontal_flip();
337  image.copy_from(*this,0,height_);
338  image.copy_from(*this,2 * width_,height_);
339  horizontal_flip();
340  }

357  inline unsigned int pixel_count() const
358  {
359  return width_ * height_;

362  inline void setwidth_height(const unsigned int width,
363  const unsigned int height,
364  const bool clear = false)
365  {
366  delete[] data_;
367  data_ = 0;
368  width_ = width;
369  height_ = height;
370 
371  create_bitmap();
372 
373  if (clear)
374  {
375  std::fill(data_,data_ + length_,0x00);
376  }
377  }
378 
379  void save_image(const std::string& file_name)
380  {
381  std::ofstream stream(file_name.c_str(),std::ios::binary);
382 
383  if (!stream)
384  {
385  std::cout << "bitmap_image::save_image(): Error - Could not open file " << file_name << " for writing!" << std::endl;
386  return;
387  }
388 
389  bitmap_file_header bfh;
390  bitmap_information_header bih;
391 
392  bih.width = width_;
393  bih.height = height_;
394  bih.bit_count = static_cast<unsigned short>(bytes_per_pixel_ << 3);
395  bih.clr_important = 0;
396  bih.clr_used = 0;
397  bih.compression = 0;
398  bih.planes = 1;
399  bih.size = 40;
400  bih.x_pels_per_meter = 0;
401  bih.y_pels_per_meter = 0;
402  bih.size_image = (((bih.width * bytes_per_pixel_) + 3) & 0x0000FFFC) * bih.height;
403 
404  bfh.type = 19778;
405  bfh.size = 55 + bih.size_image;
406  bfh.reserved1 = 0;
407  bfh.reserved2 = 0;
408  bfh.off_bits = bih.struct_size() + bfh.struct_size();
409 
410  write_bfh(stream,bfh);
411  write_bih(stream,bih);
412 
413  unsigned int padding = (4 - ((3 * width_) % 4)) % 4;
414  char padding_data[4] = {0x0,0x0,0x0,0x0};
415 
416  for (unsigned int i = 0; i < height_; ++i)
417  {
418  unsigned char* data_ptr = data_ + (row_increment_ * (height_ - i - 1));
419  stream.write(reinterpret_cast<char*>(data_ptr),sizeof(unsigned char) * bytes_per_pixel_ * width_);
420  stream.write(padding_data,padding);
421  }
422 
423  stream.close();
424  }
425 
426  inline void set_all_ith_bits_low(const unsigned int bitr_index)
427  {
428  unsigned char mask = static_cast<unsigned char>(~(1 << bitr_index));
429 
430  for (unsigned char* itr = data_; itr != data_ + length_; ++itr)
431  {
432  *itr &= mask;
433  }
434  }
435 
436  inline void set_all_ith_bits_high(const unsigned int bitr_index)
437  {
438  unsigned char mask = static_cast<unsigned char>(1 << bitr_index);
439 
440  for (unsigned char* itr = data_; itr != data_ + length_; ++itr)
441  {
442  *itr |= mask;
443  }
444  }
445 
446  inline void set_all_ith_channels(const unsigned int& channel, const unsigned char& value)
447  {
448  for (unsigned char* itr = (data_ + channel); itr < (data_ + length_); itr += bytes_per_pixel_)
449  {
450  *itr = value;
451  }
452  }

454  inline void set_channel(const color_plane color,const unsigned char& value)
455  {
456  for (unsigned char* itr = (data_ + offset(color)); itr < (data_ + length_); itr += bytes_per_pixel_)
457  {
458  *itr = value;
459  }
460  }
461 
462  inline void ror_channel(const color_plane color, const unsigned int& ror)
463  {
464  for (unsigned char* itr = (data_ + offset(color)); itr < (data_ + length_); itr += bytes_per_pixel_)
465  {
466  *itr = static_cast<unsigned char>(((*itr) >> ror) | ((*itr) << (8 - ror)));
467  }
468  }
469 
470  inline void set_all_channels(const unsigned char& value)
471  {
472  for (unsigned char* itr = data_; itr < (data_ + length_); )
473  {
474  *(itr++) = value;
475  }
476  }
477 
478  inline void set_all_channels(const unsigned char& r_value,
479  const unsigned char& g_value,
480  const unsigned char& b_value)
481  {
482  for (unsigned char* itr = (data_ + 0); itr < (data_ + length_); itr += bytes_per_pixel_)
483  {
484  *(itr + 0) = b_value;
485  *(itr + 1) = g_value;
486  *(itr + 2) = r_value;
487  }
488  }

490  inline void invert_color_planes()
491  {
492  for (unsigned char* itr = data_; itr < (data_ + length_); *itr = ~(*itr), ++itr);
493  }
494 
495  inline void add_to_color_plane(const color_plane color,const unsigned char& value)
496  {
497  for (unsigned char* itr = (data_ + offset(color)); itr < (data_ + length_); (*itr) += value, itr += bytes_per_pixel_);
498  }
499 
500  inline void convert_to_grayscale()
501  {
502  double r_scaler = 0.299;
503  double g_scaler = 0.587;
504  double b_scaler = 0.114;
505 
506  if (rgb_mode == channel_mode_)
507  {
508  double tmp = r_scaler;
509  r_scaler = b_scaler;
510  b_scaler = tmp;
511  }
512 
513  for (unsigned char* itr = data_; itr < (data_ + length_); )
514  {
515  unsigned char gray_value = static_cast<unsigned char>((r_scaler * (*(itr + 2))) +
516  (g_scaler * (*(itr + 1))) +
517  (b_scaler * (*(itr + 0))) );
518  *(itr++) = gray_value;
519  *(itr++) = gray_value;
520  *(itr++) = gray_value;
521  }
522  }
523 
524  inline const unsigned char* data()
525  {
526  return data_;
527  }
528 
529  inline void bgr_to_rgb()
530  {
531  if ((bgr_mode == channel_mode_) && (3 == bytes_per_pixel_))
532  {
533  reverse_channels();
534  channel_mode_ = rgb_mode;
535  }
536  }
537 
538  inline void rgb_to_bgr()
539  {
540  if ((rgb_mode == channel_mode_) && (3 == bytes_per_pixel_))
541  {
542  reverse_channels();
543  channel_mode_ = bgr_mode;
544  }
545  }
546 
547  inline void reverse()
548  {
549  unsigned char* itr1 = data_;
550  unsigned char* itr2 = (data_ + length_) - bytes_per_pixel_;
551 
552  while (itr1 < itr2)
553  {
554  for (std::size_t i = 0; i < bytes_per_pixel_; ++i)
555  {
556  unsigned char* citr1 = itr1 + i;
557  unsigned char* citr2 = itr2 + i;
558  unsigned char tmp = *citr1;
559  *citr1 = *citr2;
560  *citr2 = tmp;
561  }
562 
563  itr1 += bytes_per_pixel_;
564  itr2 -= bytes_per_pixel_;
565  }
566  }
567 
568  inline void horizontal_flip()
569  {
570  for (unsigned int y = 0; y < height_; ++y)
571  {
572  unsigned char* itr1 = row(y);
573  unsigned char* itr2 = itr1 + row_increment_ - bytes_per_pixel_;
574 
575  while (itr1 < itr2)
576  {
577  for (unsigned int i = 0; i < bytes_per_pixel_; ++i)
578  {
579  unsigned char* p1 = (itr1 + i);
580  unsigned char* p2 = (itr2 + i);
581  unsigned char tmp = *p1;
582  *p1 = *p2;
583  *p2 = tmp;
584  }
585 
586  itr1 += bytes_per_pixel_;
587  itr2 -= bytes_per_pixel_;
588  }
589  }
590  }
591 
592  inline void vertical_flip()
593  {
594  for (unsigned int y = 0; y < (height_ / 2); ++y)
595  {
596  unsigned char* itr1 = row(y);
597  unsigned char* itr2 = row(height_ - y - 1);
598 
599  for (std::size_t x = 0; x < row_increment_; ++x)
600  {
601  unsigned char tmp = *(itr1 + x);
602  *(itr1 + x) = *(itr2 + x);
603  *(itr2 + x) = tmp;
604  }
605  }
606  }
607 
608  inline void export_color_plane(const color_plane color, unsigned char* image)
609  {
610  for (unsigned char* itr = (data_ + offset(color)); itr < (data_ + length_); ++image, itr += bytes_per_pixel_)
611  {
612  (*image) = (*itr);
613  }
614  }
615 
616  inline void export_color_plane(const color_plane color, bitmap_image& image)
617  {
618  if (
619  (width_ != image.width_ ) ||
620  (height_ != image.height_)
621  )
622  {
623  image.setwidth_height(width_,height_);
624  }
625 
626  image.clear();
627 
628  unsigned char* itr1 = (data_ + offset(color));
629  unsigned char* itr1_end = (data_ + length_);
630  unsigned char* itr2 = (image.data_ + offset(color));
631 
632  while (itr1 < itr1_end)
633  {
634  (*itr2) = (*itr1);
635  itr1 += bytes_per_pixel_;
636  itr2 += bytes_per_pixel_;
637  }
638  }
639 
640  inline void export_response_image(const color_plane color, double* response_image)
641  {
642  for (unsigned char* itr = (data_ + offset(color)); itr < (data_ + length_); ++response_image, itr += bytes_per_pixel_)
643  {
644  (*response_image) = (1.0 * (*itr)) / 256.0;
645  }
646  }
647 
648  inline void export_gray_scale_response_image(double* response_image)
649  {
650  for (unsigned char* itr = data_; itr < (data_ + length_); itr += bytes_per_pixel_)
651  {
652  unsigned char gray_value = static_cast<unsigned char>((0.299 * (*(itr + 2))) +
653  (0.587 * (*(itr + 1))) +
654  (0.114 * (*(itr + 0))));
655  (*response_image) = (1.0 * gray_value) / 256.0;
656  }
657  }
658 
659  inline void export_rgb(double* red, double* green, double* blue) const
660  {
661  if (bgr_mode != channel_mode_)
662  return;
663 
664  for (unsigned char* itr = data_; itr < (data_ + length_); ++red, ++green, ++blue)
665  {
666  (*blue) = (1.0 * (*(itr++))) / 256.0;
667  (*green) = (1.0 * (*(itr++))) / 256.0;
668  (*red) = (1.0 * (*(itr++))) / 256.0;
669  }
670  }
671 
672  inline void export_rgb(float* red, float* green, float* blue) const
673  {
674  if (bgr_mode != channel_mode_)
675  return;
676 
677  for (unsigned char* itr = data_; itr < (data_ + length_); ++red, ++green, ++blue)
678  {
679  (*blue) = (1.0f * (*(itr++))) / 256.0f;
680  (*green) = (1.0f * (*(itr++))) / 256.0f;
681  (*red) = (1.0f * (*(itr++))) / 256.0f;
682  }
683  }
684 
685  inline void export_rgb(unsigned char* red, unsigned char* green, unsigned char* blue) const
686  {
687  if (bgr_mode != channel_mode_)
688  return;
689 
690  for (unsigned char* itr = data_; itr < (data_ + length_); ++red, ++green, ++blue)
691  {
692  (*blue) = *(itr++);
693  (*green) = *(itr++);
694  (*red) = *(itr++);
695  }
696  }
697 
698  inline void export_ycbcr(double* y, double* cb, double* cr)
699  {
700  if (bgr_mode != channel_mode_)
701  return;
702 
703  for (unsigned char* itr = data_; itr < (data_ + length_); ++y, ++cb, ++cr)
704  {
705  double blue = (1.0 * (*(itr++)));
706  double green = (1.0 * (*(itr++)));
707  double red = (1.0 * (*(itr++)));
708 
709  ( *y) = clamp<double>( 16.0 + (1.0/256.0) * ( 65.738 * red + 129.057 * green + 25.064 * blue),1.0,254);
710  (*cb) = clamp<double>(128.0 + (1.0/256.0) * (- 37.945 * red - 74.494 * green + 112.439 * blue),1.0,254);
711  (*cr) = clamp<double>(128.0 + (1.0/256.0) * ( 112.439 * red - 94.154 * green - 18.285 * blue),1.0,254);
712  }
713  }
714 
715  inline void export_rgb_normal(double* red, double* green, double* blue) const
716  {
717  if (bgr_mode != channel_mode_)
718  return;
719 
720  for (unsigned char* itr = data_; itr < (data_ + length_); ++red, ++green, ++blue)
721  {
722  (*blue) = (1.0 * (*(itr++)));
723  (*green) = (1.0 * (*(itr++)));
724  (*red) = (1.0 * (*(itr++)));
725  }
726  }
727 
728  inline void export_rgb_normal(float* red, float* green, float* blue) const
729  {
730  if (bgr_mode != channel_mode_)
731  return;
732 
733  for (unsigned char* itr = data_; itr < (data_ + length_); ++red, ++green, ++blue)
734  {
735  (*blue) = (1.0f * (*(itr++)));
736  (*green) = (1.0f * (*(itr++)));
737  (*red) = (1.0f * (*(itr++)));
738  }
739  }

749  *(itr++) = static_cast<unsigned char>(256.0 * (*green));

751  }

792  *(itr++) = static_cast<unsigned char>(clamp((298.082 * y_ - 100.291 * cb_ - 208.120 * cr_ ) / 256.0 + 135.576,0.0,255.0));
793  *(itr++) = static_cast<unsigned char>(clamp((298.082 * y_ + 408.583 * cr_ ) / 256.0 - 222.921,0.0,255.0));

848 
849  inline void subsample(bitmap_image& dest)
850  {
851  /*
852  Half sub-sample of original image.
853  */
854  unsigned int w = 0;
855  unsigned int h = 0;
856 
857  bool odd_width = false;
858  bool odd_height = false;
859 
860  if (0 == (width_ % 2))
861  w = width_ / 2;
862  else
863  {
864  w = 1 + (width_ / 2);
865  odd_width = true;
866  }
867 
868  if (0 == (height_ % 2))
869  h = height_ / 2;
870  else
871  {
872  h = 1 + (height_ / 2);
873  odd_height = true;
874  }
875 
876  unsigned int horizontal_upper = (odd_width) ? (w - 1) : w;
877  unsigned int vertical_upper = (odd_height) ? (h - 1) : h;
878 
879  dest.setwidth_height(w,h);
880  dest.clear();
881 
882  unsigned char* s_itr[3];
883  const unsigned char* itr1[3];
884  const unsigned char* itr2[3];
885 
886  s_itr[0] = dest.data_ + 0;
887  s_itr[1] = dest.data_ + 1;
888  s_itr[2] = dest.data_ + 2;
889 
890  itr1[0] = data_ + 0;
891  itr1[1] = data_ + 1;
892  itr1[2] = data_ + 2;
893 
894  itr2[0] = data_ + row_increment_ + 0;
895  itr2[1] = data_ + row_increment_ + 1;
896  itr2[2] = data_ + row_increment_ + 2;
897 
898  unsigned int total = 0;
899 
900  for (unsigned int j = 0; j < vertical_upper; ++j)
901  {
902  for (unsigned int i = 0; i < horizontal_upper; ++i)
903  {
904  for (unsigned int k = 0; k < bytes_per_pixel_; s_itr[k] += bytes_per_pixel_, ++k)
905  {
906  total = 0;
907  total += *(itr1[k]); itr1[k] += bytes_per_pixel_;
908  total += *(itr1[k]); itr1[k] += bytes_per_pixel_;
909  total += *(itr2[k]); itr2[k] += bytes_per_pixel_;
910  total += *(itr2[k]); itr2[k] += bytes_per_pixel_;
911 
912  *(s_itr[k]) = static_cast<unsigned char>(total >> 2);
913  }
914  }
915 
916  if (odd_width)
917  {
918  for (unsigned int k = 0; k < bytes_per_pixel_; s_itr[k] += bytes_per_pixel_, ++k)
919  {
920  total = 0;
921  total += *(itr1[k]); itr1[k] += bytes_per_pixel_;
922  total += *(itr2[k]); itr2[k] += bytes_per_pixel_;
923 
924  *(s_itr[k]) = static_cast<unsigned char>(total >> 1);
925  }
926  }
927 
928  for (unsigned int k = 0; k < bytes_per_pixel_; itr1[k] += row_increment_, ++k);
929 
930  if (j != (vertical_upper - 1))
931  {
932  for (unsigned int k = 0; k < bytes_per_pixel_; itr2[k] += row_increment_, ++k);
933  }
934  }
935 
936  if (odd_height)
937  {
938  for (unsigned int i = 0; i < horizontal_upper; ++i)
939  {
940  for (unsigned int k = 0; k < bytes_per_pixel_; s_itr[k] += bytes_per_pixel_, ++k)
941  {
942  total = 0;
943  total += *(itr1[k]); itr1[k] += bytes_per_pixel_;
944  total += *(itr2[k]); itr2[k] += bytes_per_pixel_;
945 
946  *(s_itr[k]) = static_cast<unsigned char>(total >> 1);
947  }
948  }
949 
950  if (odd_width)
951  {
952  for (unsigned int k = 0; k < bytes_per_pixel_; ++k)
953  {
954  (*(s_itr[k])) = *(itr1[k]);
955  }
956  }
957  }
958  }
959 
960  inline void upsample(bitmap_image& dest)
961  {
962  /*
963  2x up-sample of original image.
964  */
965 
966  dest.setwidth_height(2 * width_ ,2 * height_);
967  dest.clear();
968 
969  const unsigned char* s_itr[3];
970  unsigned char* itr1[3];
971  unsigned char* itr2[3];
972 
973  s_itr[0] = data_ + 0;
974  s_itr[1] = data_ + 1;
975  s_itr[2] = data_ + 2;
976 
977  itr1[0] = dest.data_ + 0;
978  itr1[1] = dest.data_ + 1;
979  itr1[2] = dest.data_ + 2;
980 
981  itr2[0] = dest.data_ + dest.row_increment_ + 0;
982  itr2[1] = dest.data_ + dest.row_increment_ + 1;
983  itr2[2] = dest.data_ + dest.row_increment_ + 2;
984 
985  for (unsigned int j = 0; j < height_; ++j)
986  {
987  for (unsigned int i = 0; i < width_; ++i)
988  {
989  for (unsigned int k = 0; k < bytes_per_pixel_; s_itr[k] += bytes_per_pixel_, ++k)
990  {
991  *(itr1[k]) = *(s_itr[k]); itr1[k] += bytes_per_pixel_;
992  *(itr1[k]) = *(s_itr[k]); itr1[k] += bytes_per_pixel_;
993 
994  *(itr2[k]) = *(s_itr[k]); itr2[k] += bytes_per_pixel_;
995  *(itr2[k]) = *(s_itr[k]); itr2[k] += bytes_per_pixel_;
996  }
997  }
998 
999  for (unsigned int k = 0; k < bytes_per_pixel_; ++k)
1000  {
1001  itr1[k] += dest.row_increment_;
1002  itr2[k] += dest.row_increment_;
1003  }
1004  }
1005  }
1006 
1007  inline void alpha_blend(const double& alpha, const bitmap_image& image)
1008  {
1009  if (
1010  (image.width_ != width_ ) ||
1011  (image.height_ != height_)
1012  )
1013  {
1014  return;
1015  }
1016 
1017  if ((alpha < 0.0) || (alpha > 1.0))
1018  {
1019  return;
1020  }
1021 
1022  unsigned char* itr1 = data_;
1023  unsigned char* itr1_end = data_ + length_;
1024  unsigned char* itr2 = image.data_;
1025 
1026  double alpha_compliment = 1.0 - alpha;
1027 
1028  while (itr1 != itr1_end)
1029  {
1030  *(itr1) = static_cast<unsigned char>((alpha * (*itr2)) + (alpha_compliment * (*itr1)));
1031  ++itr1;
1032  ++itr2;
1033  }
1034  }
1035 
1036  inline double psnr(const bitmap_image& image)
1037  {
1038  if (
1039  (image.width_ != width_ ) ||
1040  (image.height_ != height_)
1041  )
1042  {
1043  return 0.0;
1044  }
1045 
1046  unsigned char* itr1 = data_;
1047  unsigned char* itr2 = image.data_;
1048 
1049  double mse = 0.0;
1050 
1051  while (itr1 != (data_ + length_))
1052  {
1053  double v = (static_cast<double>(*itr1) - static_cast<double>(*itr2));
1054 
1055  mse += v * v;
1056  ++itr1;
1057  ++itr2;
1058  }
1059 
1060  if (mse <= 0.0000001)
1061  {
1062  return 1000000.0;
1063  }
1064  else
1065  {
1066  mse /= (3.0 * width_ * height_);
1067  return 20.0 * std::log10(255.0 / std::sqrt(mse));
1068  }
1069  }
1070 
1071  inline double psnr(const unsigned int& x,
1072  const unsigned int& y,
1073  const bitmap_image& image)
1074  {
1075  if ((x + image.width()) > width_) { return 0.0; }
1076  if ((y + image.height()) > height_) { return 0.0; }
1077 
1078  double mse = 0.0;
1079 
1080  const unsigned int height = image.height();
1081  const unsigned int width = image.width();
1082 
1083  for (unsigned int r = 0; r < height; ++r)
1084  {
1085  unsigned char* itr1 = row(r + y) + x * bytes_per_pixel_;
1086  unsigned char* itr1_end = itr1 + (width * bytes_per_pixel_);
1087  const unsigned char* itr2 = image.row(r);
1088 
1089  while (itr1 != itr1_end)
1090  {
1091  double v = (static_cast<double>(*itr1) - static_cast<double>(*itr2));
1092  mse += v * v;
1093  ++itr1;
1094  ++itr2;
1095  }
1096  }
1097 
1098  if (mse <= 0.0000001)
1099  {
1100  return 1000000.0;
1101  }
1102  else
1103  {
1104  mse /= (3.0 * image.width() * image.height());
1105  return 20.0 * std::log10(255.0 / std::sqrt(mse));
1106  }
1107  }
1108 
1109  inline void histogram(const color_plane color, double hist[256])
1110  {
1111  std::fill(hist,hist + 256,0.0);
1112 
1113  for (unsigned char* itr = (data_ + offset(color)); itr < (data_ + length_); itr += bytes_per_pixel_)
1114  {
1115  ++hist[(*itr)];
1116  }
1117  }
1118 
1119  inline void histogram_normalized(const color_plane color, double hist[256])
1120  {
1121  histogram(color,hist);
1122 
1123  double* h_itr = hist;
1124  const double* h_end = hist + 256;
1125  const double pixel_count = static_cast<double>(width_ * height_);
1126 
1127  while (h_end != h_itr)
1128  {
1129  *(h_itr++) /= pixel_count;
1130  }
1131  }
1132 
1133  inline unsigned int offset(const color_plane color)
1134  {
1135  switch (channel_mode_)
1136  {
1137  case rgb_mode : {
1138  switch (color)
1139  {
1140  case red_plane : return 0;
1141  case green_plane : return 1;
1142  case blue_plane : return 2;
1143  default : return std::numeric_limits<unsigned int>::max();
1144  }
1145  }
1146 
1147  case bgr_mode : {
1148  switch (color)
1149  {
1150  case red_plane : return 2;
1151  case green_plane : return 1;
1152  case blue_plane : return 0;
1153  default : return std::numeric_limits<unsigned int>::max();
1154  }
1155  }
1156 
1157  default : return std::numeric_limits<unsigned int>::max();
1158  }
1159  }
1160 
1161  inline void incremental()
1162  {
1163  unsigned char current_color = 0;
1164 
1165  for (unsigned char* itr = data_; itr < (data_ + length_);)
1166  {
1167  (*itr++) = (current_color);
1168  (*itr++) = (current_color);
1169  (*itr++) = (current_color);
1170 
1171  ++current_color;
1172  }
1173  }

1177  struct bitmap_file_header
1178  {
1179  unsigned short type;
1180  unsigned int size;
1181  unsigned short reserved1;
1182  unsigned short reserved2;
1183  unsigned int off_bits;
1184 
1185  unsigned int struct_size()
1186  {
1187  return sizeof(type) +
1188  sizeof(size) +
1189  sizeof(reserved1) +
1190  sizeof(reserved2) +
1191  sizeof(off_bits);
1192  }
1193  };
1194 
1195  struct bitmap_information_header
1196  {
1197  unsigned int size;
1198  unsigned int width;
1199  unsigned int height;
1200  unsigned short planes;
1201  unsigned short bit_count;
1202  unsigned int compression;
1203  unsigned int size_image;
1204  unsigned int x_pels_per_meter;
1205  unsigned int y_pels_per_meter;
1206  unsigned int clr_used;
1207  unsigned int clr_important;
1208 
1209  unsigned int struct_size()
1210  {
1211  return sizeof(size) +
1212  sizeof(width) +
1213  sizeof(height) +
1214  sizeof(planes) +
1215  sizeof(bit_count) +
1216  sizeof(compression) +
1217  sizeof(size_image) +
1218  sizeof(x_pels_per_meter) +
1219  sizeof(y_pels_per_meter) +
1220  sizeof(clr_used) +
1221  sizeof(clr_important);
1222  }
1223  };
1224 
1225  inline bool big_endian()
1226  {
1227  unsigned int v = 0x01;
1228 
1229  return (1 != reinterpret_cast<char*>(&v)[0]);
1230  }
1231 
1232  inline unsigned short flip(const unsigned short& v)
1233  {
1234  return ((v >> 8) | (v << 8));
1235  }
1236 
1237  inline unsigned int flip(const unsigned int& v)
1238  {
1239  return (((v & 0xFF000000) >> 0x18) |
1240  ((v & 0x000000FF) << 0x18) |
1241  ((v & 0x00FF0000) >> 0x08) |
1242  ((v & 0x0000FF00) << 0x08));
1243  }
1244 
1245  template<typename T>
1246  inline void read_from_stream(std::ifstream& stream,T& t)
1247  {
1248  stream.read(reinterpret_cast<char*>(&t),sizeof(T));
1249  }
1250 
1251  template<typename T>
1252  inline void write_to_stream(std::ofstream& stream,const T& t)
1253  {
1254  stream.write(reinterpret_cast<const char*>(&t),sizeof(T));
1255  }
1256 
1257  inline void read_bfh(std::ifstream& stream, bitmap_file_header& bfh)
1258  {
1259  read_from_stream(stream,bfh.type);
1260  read_from_stream(stream,bfh.size);
1261  read_from_stream(stream,bfh.reserved1);
1262  read_from_stream(stream,bfh.reserved2);
1263  read_from_stream(stream,bfh.off_bits);
1264 
1265  if (big_endian())
1266  {
1267  bfh.type = flip(bfh.type);
1268  bfh.size = flip(bfh.size);
1269  bfh.reserved1 = flip(bfh.reserved1);
1270  bfh.reserved2 = flip(bfh.reserved2);
1271  bfh.off_bits = flip(bfh.off_bits);
1272  }
1273  }
1274 
1275  inline void write_bfh(std::ofstream& stream, const bitmap_file_header& bfh)
1276  {
1277  if (big_endian())
1278  {
1279  write_to_stream(stream,flip(bfh.type ));
1280  write_to_stream(stream,flip(bfh.size ));
1281  write_to_stream(stream,flip(bfh.reserved1));
1282  write_to_stream(stream,flip(bfh.reserved2));
1283  write_to_stream(stream,flip(bfh.off_bits ));
1284  }
1285  else
1286  {
1287  write_to_stream(stream,bfh.type );
1288  write_to_stream(stream,bfh.size );
1289  write_to_stream(stream,bfh.reserved1);
1290  write_to_stream(stream,bfh.reserved2);
1291  write_to_stream(stream,bfh.off_bits );
1292  }
1293  }
1294 
1295  inline void read_bih(std::ifstream& stream,bitmap_information_header& bih)
1296  {
1297  read_from_stream(stream,bih.size );
1298  read_from_stream(stream,bih.width );
1299  read_from_stream(stream,bih.height);
1300  read_from_stream(stream,bih.planes);
1301  read_from_stream(stream,bih.bit_count);
1302  read_from_stream(stream,bih.compression);
1303  read_from_stream(stream,bih.size_image);
1304  read_from_stream(stream,bih.x_pels_per_meter);
1305  read_from_stream(stream,bih.y_pels_per_meter);
1306  read_from_stream(stream,bih.clr_used);
1307  read_from_stream(stream,bih.clr_important);
1308 
1309  if (big_endian())
1310  {
1311  bih.size = flip(bih.size );
1312  bih.width = flip(bih.width );
1313  bih.height = flip(bih.height );
1314  bih.planes = flip(bih.planes );
1315  bih.bit_count = flip(bih.bit_count);
1316  bih.compression = flip(bih.compression);
1317  bih.size_image = flip(bih.size_image);
1318  bih.x_pels_per_meter = flip(bih.x_pels_per_meter);
1319  bih.y_pels_per_meter = flip(bih.y_pels_per_meter);
1320  bih.clr_used = flip(bih.clr_used);
1321  bih.clr_important = flip(bih.clr_important);
1322  }
1323  }
1324 
1325  inline void write_bih(std::ofstream& stream, const bitmap_information_header& bih)
1326  {
1327  if (big_endian())
1328  {
1329  write_to_stream(stream,flip(bih.size));
1330  write_to_stream(stream,flip(bih.width));
1331  write_to_stream(stream,flip(bih.height));
1332  write_to_stream(stream,flip(bih.planes));
1333  write_to_stream(stream,flip(bih.bit_count));
1334  write_to_stream(stream,flip(bih.compression));
1335  write_to_stream(stream,flip(bih.size_image));
1336  write_to_stream(stream,flip(bih.x_pels_per_meter));
1337  write_to_stream(stream,flip(bih.y_pels_per_meter));
1338  write_to_stream(stream,flip(bih.clr_used));
1339  write_to_stream(stream,flip(bih.clr_important));
1340  }
1341  else
1342  {
1343  write_to_stream(stream,bih.size);
1344  write_to_stream(stream,bih.width);
1345  write_to_stream(stream,bih.height);
1346  write_to_stream(stream,bih.planes);
1347  write_to_stream(stream,bih.bit_count);
1348  write_to_stream(stream,bih.compression);
1349  write_to_stream(stream,bih.size_image);
1350  write_to_stream(stream,bih.x_pels_per_meter);
1351  write_to_stream(stream,bih.y_pels_per_meter);
1352  write_to_stream(stream,bih.clr_used);
1353  write_to_stream(stream,bih.clr_important);
1354  }
1355  }
1356 
1357  void create_bitmap()
1358  {
1359  length_ = width_ * height_ * bytes_per_pixel_;
1360  row_increment_ = width_ * bytes_per_pixel_;
1361 
1362  if (0 != data_)
1363  {
1364  delete[] data_;
1365  }
1366 
1367  data_ = new unsigned char[length_];
1368  }
1369 
1370  void load_bitmap()
1371  {
1372  std::ifstream stream(file_name_.c_str(),std::ios::binary);
1373 
1374  if (!stream)
1375  {
1376  std::cerr << "bitmap_image::load_bitmap() ERROR: bitmap_image - file " << file_name_ << " not found!" << std::endl;
1377  return;
1378  }
1379 
1380  bitmap_file_header bfh;
1381  bitmap_information_header bih;
1382 
1383  read_bfh(stream,bfh);
1384  read_bih(stream,bih);
1385 
1386  if (bfh.type != 19778)
1387  {
1388  stream.close();
1389  std::cerr << "bitmap_image::load_bitmap() ERROR: bitmap_image - Invalid type value " << bfh.type << " expected 19778." << std::endl;
1390  return;
1391  }
1392 
1393  if (bih.bit_count != 24)
1394  {
1395  stream.close();
1396  std::cerr << "bitmap_image::load_bitmap() ERROR: bitmap_image - Invalid bit depth " << bih.bit_count << " expected 24." << std::endl;
1397 
1398  return;
1399  }
1400 
1401  height_ = bih.height;
1402  width_ = bih.width;
1403 
1404  bytes_per_pixel_ = bih.bit_count >> 3;
1405 
1406  unsigned int padding = (4 - ((3 * width_) % 4)) % 4;
1407  char padding_data[4] = {0,0,0,0};
1408 
1409  create_bitmap();
1410 
1411  for (unsigned int i = 0; i < height_; ++i)
1412  {
1413  unsigned char* data_ptr = row(height_ - i - 1); // read in inverted row order
1414 
1415  stream.read(reinterpret_cast<char*>(data_ptr),sizeof(char) * bytes_per_pixel_ * width_);
1416  stream.read(padding_data,padding);
1417  }
1418  }
1419 
1420  inline void reverse_channels()
1421  {
1422  if (3 != bytes_per_pixel_)
1423  return;
1424 
1425  for (unsigned char* itr = data_; itr < (data_ + length_); itr += bytes_per_pixel_)
1426  {
1427  unsigned char tmp = *(itr + 0);
1428 
1429  *(itr + 0) = *(itr + 2);
1430  *(itr + 2) = tmp;
1431  }
1432  }
1433 
1434  template<typename T>
1435  inline T clamp(const T& v, const T& lower_range, const T& upper_range)
1436  {
1437  if (v < lower_range)
1438  return lower_range;
1439  else if (v > upper_range)
1440  return upper_range;
1441  else
1442  return v;
1443  }
1444 
1445  std::string file_name_;
1446  unsigned char* data_;
1447  unsigned int length_;
1448  unsigned int width_;
1449  unsigned int height_;
1450  unsigned int row_increment_;
1451  unsigned int bytes_per_pixel_;
1452  channel_mode channel_mode_;
1453 };

1456 struct rgb_store
1457 {
1458  unsigned char red;
1459  unsigned char green;
1460  unsigned char blue;
1461 };
1462 
1463 inline void rgb_to_ycbcr(const unsigned int& length, double* red, double* green, double* blue,
1464  double* y, double* cb, double* cr)
1465 {
1466  unsigned int i = 0;
1467 
1468  while (i < length)
1469  {
1470  ( *y) = 16.0 + ( 65.481 * (*red) + 128.553 * (*green) + 24.966 * (*blue));
1471  (*cb) = 128.0 + ( -37.797 * (*red) + -74.203 * (*green) + 112.000 * (*blue));
1472  (*cr) = 128.0 + ( 112.000 * (*red) + -93.786 * (*green) - 18.214 * (*blue));
1473 
1474  ++i;
1475  ++red; ++green; ++blue;
1476  ++y; ++cb; ++cr;
1477  }
1478 }
1479 
1480 inline void ycbcr_to_rgb(const unsigned int& length, double* y, double* cb, double* cr,
1481  double* red, double* green, double* blue)
1482 {
1483  unsigned int i = 0;
1484 
1485  while (i < length)
1486  {
1487  double y_ = (*y) - 16.0;
1488  double cb_ = (*cb) - 128.0;
1489  double cr_ = (*cr) - 128.0;
1490 
1491  (*red) = 0.000456621 * y_ + 0.00625893 * cr_;
1492  (*green) = 0.000456621 * y_ - 0.00153632 * cb_ - 0.00318811 * cr_;
1493  (*blue) = 0.000456621 * y_ + 0.00791071 * cb_;
1494 
1495  ++i;
1496  ++red; ++green; ++blue;
1497  ++y; ++cb; ++cr;
1498  }
1499 }
1500 
1501 inline void subsample(const unsigned int& width,
1502  const unsigned int& height,
1503  const double* source,
1504  unsigned int& w,
1505  unsigned int& h,
1506  double** dest)
1507 {
1508  /* Single channel. */
1509 
1510  w = 0;
1511  h = 0;
1512 
1513  bool odd_width = false;
1514  bool odd_height = false;
1515 
1516  if (0 == (width % 2))
1517  w = width / 2;
1518  else
1519  {
1520  w = 1 + (width / 2);
1521  odd_width = true;
1522  }
1523 
1524  if (0 == (height % 2))
1525  h = height / 2;
1526  else
1527  {
1528  h = 1 + (height / 2);
1529  odd_height = true;
1530  }
1531 
1532  unsigned int horizontal_upper = (odd_width) ? w - 1 : w;
1533  unsigned int vertical_upper = (odd_height) ? h - 1 : h;
1534 
1535  *dest = new double[w * h];
1536 
1537  double* s_itr = *dest;
1538  const double* itr1 = source;
1539  const double* itr2 = source + width;
1540 
1541  for (unsigned int j = 0; j < vertical_upper; ++j)
1542  {
1543  for (unsigned int i = 0; i < horizontal_upper; ++i, ++s_itr)
1544  {
1545  (*s_itr) = *(itr1++);
1546  (*s_itr) += *(itr1++);
1547  (*s_itr) += *(itr2++);
1548  (*s_itr) += *(itr2++);
1549  (*s_itr) /= 4.0;
1550  }
1551 
1552  if (odd_width)
1553  {
1554  (*(s_itr++)) = ( (*itr1++) + (*itr2++) ) / 2.0;
1555  }
1556 
1557  itr1 += width;
1558 
1559  if (j != (vertical_upper -1))
1560  {
1561  itr2 += width;
1562  }
1563  }
1564 
1565  if (odd_height)
1566  {
1567  for (unsigned int i = 0; i < horizontal_upper; ++i, ++s_itr)
1568  {
1569  (*s_itr) += (*(itr1++));
1570  (*s_itr) += (*(itr1++));
1571  (*s_itr) /= 2.0;
1572  }
1573 
1574  if (odd_width)
1575  {
1576  (*(s_itr++)) = (*itr1);
1577  }
1578  }
1579 }
1580 
1581 inline void upsample(const unsigned int& width,
1582  const unsigned int& height,
1583  const double* source,
1584  unsigned int& w,
1585  unsigned int& h,
1586  double** dest)
1587 {
1588  /* Single channel. */
1589 
1590  w = 2 * width;
1591  h = 2 * height;
1592 
1593  *dest = new double[w * h];
1594 
1595  const double* s_itr = source;
1596  double* itr1 = *dest;
1597  double* itr2 = *dest + w;
1598 
1599  for (unsigned int j = 0; j < height; ++j)
1600  {
1601  for (unsigned int i = 0; i < width; ++i, ++s_itr)
1602  {
1603  *(itr1++) = (*s_itr);
1604  *(itr1++) = (*s_itr);
1605  *(itr2++) = (*s_itr);
1606  *(itr2++) = (*s_itr);
1607  }
1608 
1609  itr1 += w;
1610  itr2 += w;
1611  }
1612 }

1614 inline void checkered_pattern(const unsigned int x_width,
1615  const unsigned int y_width,
1616  const unsigned char value,
1617  const bitmap_image::color_plane color,
1618  bitmap_image& image)
1619 {
1620  if (
1621  (x_width >= image.width ()) ||
1622  (y_width >= image.height())
1623  )
1624  {
1625  return;
1626  }
1627 
1628  bool setter_x = false;
1629  bool setter_y = true;
1630 
1631  const unsigned int color_plane_offset = image.offset(color);
1632  const unsigned int height = image.height();
1633  const unsigned int width = image.width();
1634 
1635  for (unsigned int y = 0; y < height; ++y)
1636  {
1637  if (0 == (y % y_width))
1638  {
1639  setter_y = !setter_y;
1640  }
1641 
1642  unsigned char* row = image.row(y) + color_plane_offset;
1643 
1644  for (unsigned int x = 0; x < width; ++x, row += image.bytes_per_pixel())
1645  {
1646  if (0 == (x % x_width))
1647  {
1648  setter_x = !setter_x;
1649  }
1650 
1651  if (setter_x ^ setter_y)
1652  {
1653  *row = value;
1654  }
1655  }
1656  }
1657 }

1659 inline void checkered_pattern(const unsigned int x_width,
1660  const unsigned int y_width,
1661  const unsigned char red,
1662  const unsigned char green,
1663  const unsigned char blue,
1664  bitmap_image& image)
1665 {
1666  if (
1667  (x_width >= image.width ()) ||
1668  (y_width >= image.height())
1669  )
1670  {
1671  return;
1672  }
1673 
1674  bool setter_x = false;
1675  bool setter_y = true;
1676 
1677  const unsigned int height = image.height();
1678  const unsigned int width = image.width();
1679 
1680  for (unsigned int y = 0; y < height; ++y)
1681  {
1682  if (0 == (y % y_width))
1683  {
1684  setter_y = !setter_y;
1685  }
1686 
1687  unsigned char* row = image.row(y);
1688 
1689  for (unsigned int x = 0; x < width; ++x, row += image.bytes_per_pixel())
1690  {
1691  if (0 == (x % x_width))
1692  {
1693  setter_x = !setter_x;
1694  }
1695

1697  {
1698  *(row + 0) = blue;
1699  *(row + 1) = green;
1700  *(row + 2) = red;
1701  }
1702  }
1703  }

1706 inline void plasma(bitmap_image& image,
1707  const double& x, const double& y,
1708  const double& width, const double& height,
1709  const double& c1, const double& c2,
1710  const double& c3, const double& c4,
1711  const double& roughness = 3.0,
1712  const rgb_store colormap[] = 0)
1713 {
1714  // Note: c1,c2,c3,c4 -> [0.0,1.0]
1715 
1716  double half_width = ( width / 2.0);
1717  double half_height = (height / 2.0);
1718 
1719  if ((width >= 1.0) || (height >= 1.0))
1720  {
1721  double corner1 = (c1 + c2) / 2.0;
1722  double corner2 = (c2 + c3) / 2.0;
1723  double corner3 = (c3 + c4) / 2.0;
1724  double corner4 = (c4 + c1) / 2.0;
1725  double center = (c1 + c2 + c3 + c4) / 4.0 +
1726  ((1.0 * ::rand() /(1.0 * RAND_MAX)) - 0.5) * // should use a better rng
1727  ((1.0 * half_width + half_height) / (image.width() + image.height()) * roughness);
1728 
1729  center = std::min<double>(std::max<double>(0.0,center),1.0);
1730 
1731  plasma(image, x, y, half_width, half_height, c1, corner1, center, corner4,roughness,colormap);
1732  plasma(image, x + half_width, y, half_width, half_height, corner1, c2, corner2, center,roughness,colormap);
1733  plasma(image, x + half_width, y + half_height, half_width, half_height, center, corner2, c3, corner3,roughness,colormap);
1734  plasma(image, x, y + half_height, half_width, half_height, corner4, center, corner3, c4,roughness,colormap);
1735  }
1736  else
1737  {
1738  rgb_store color = colormap[static_cast<unsigned int>(1000.0 * ((c1 + c2 + c3 + c4) / 4.0)) % 1000];
1739  image.set_pixel(static_cast<unsigned int>(x),static_cast<unsigned int>(y),color.red,color.green,color.blue);
1740  }
1741 }
1742 
1743 inline double psnr_region(const unsigned int& x, const unsigned int& y,
1744  const unsigned int& width, const unsigned int& height,
1745  const bitmap_image& image1, const bitmap_image& image2)
1746 {
1747  if (
1748  (image1.width() != image2.width ()) ||
1749  (image1.height() != image2.height())
1750  )
1751  {
1752  return 0.0;
1753  }
1754 
1755  if ((x + width) > image1.width()) { return 0.0; }
1756  if ((y + height) > image1.height()) { return 0.0; }
1757 
1758  double mse = 0.0;
1759 
1760  for (unsigned int r = 0; r < height; ++r)
1761  {
1762  const unsigned char* itr1 = image1.row(r + y) + x * image1.bytes_per_pixel();
1763  const unsigned char* itr1_end = itr1 + (width * image1.bytes_per_pixel());
1764  const unsigned char* itr2 = image2.row(r + y) + x * image2.bytes_per_pixel();
1765 
1766  while (itr1 != itr1_end)
1767  {
1768  double v = (static_cast<double>(*itr1) - static_cast<double>(*itr2));
1769  mse += v * v;
1770  ++itr1;
1771  ++itr2;
1772  }
1773  }
1774 
1775  if (mse <= 0.0000001)
1776  {
1777  return 1000000.0;
1778  }
1779  else
1780  {
1781  mse /= (3.0 * width * height);
1782  return 20.0 * std::log10(255.0 / std::sqrt(mse));
1783  }
1784 }
1785 
1786 inline void hierarchical_psnr_r(const double& x, const double& y,
1787  const double& width, const double& height,
1788  const bitmap_image& image1,
1789  bitmap_image& image2,
1790  const double& threshold,
1791  const rgb_store colormap[])
1792 {
1793  if ((width <= 4.0) || (height <= 4.0))
1794  {
1795  double psnr = psnr_region(static_cast<unsigned int>(x),
1796  static_cast<unsigned int>(y),
1797  static_cast<unsigned int>(width),
1798  static_cast<unsigned int>(height),
1799  image1,image2);
1800 
1801  if (psnr < threshold)
1802  {
1803  rgb_store c = colormap[static_cast<unsigned int>(1000.0 * (1.0 - (psnr / threshold)))];
1804  image2.set_region(static_cast<unsigned int>(x),
1805  static_cast<unsigned int>(y),
1806  static_cast<unsigned int>(width + 1),
1807  static_cast<unsigned int>(height + 1),
1808  c.red,c.green,c.blue);
1809  }
1810  }
1811  else
1812  {
1813  double half_width = ( width / 2.0);
1814  double half_height = (height / 2.0);
1815 
1816  hierarchical_psnr_r(x , y , half_width, half_height,image1,image2,threshold,colormap);
1817  hierarchical_psnr_r(x + half_width, y , half_width, half_height,image1,image2,threshold,colormap);
1818  hierarchical_psnr_r(x + half_width, y + half_height, half_width, half_height,image1,image2,threshold,colormap);
1819  hierarchical_psnr_r(x , y + half_height, half_width, half_height,image1,image2,threshold,colormap);
1820  }
1821 }
1822 
1823 inline void hierarchical_psnr(bitmap_image& image1,bitmap_image& image2, const double threshold, const rgb_store colormap[])
1824 {
1825  if (
1826  (image1.width() != image2.width ()) ||
1827  (image1.height() != image2.height())
1828  )
1829  {
1830  return;
1831  }
1832 
1833  double psnr = psnr_region(0,0,image1.width(),image1.height(),image1,image2);
1834 
1835  if (psnr < threshold)
1836  {
1837  hierarchical_psnr_r(0,0, image1.width(), image1.height(),image1,image2,threshold,colormap);
1838  }
1839 }

1868  void quadix(int x1, int y1, int x2, int y2,int x3, int y3, int x4, int y4)
1869  {
1870  line_segment(x1,y1,x2,y2);
1871  line_segment(x2,y2,x3,y3);

1875 
1876  void line_segment(int x1, int y1, int x2, int y2)
1877  {
1878  int steep = 0;
1879  int sx = ((x2 - x1) > 0) ? 1 : -1;
1880  int sy = ((y2 - y1) > 0) ? 1 : -1;
1881  int dx = abs(x2 - x1);
1882  int dy = abs(y2 - y1);
1883 
1884  if (dy > dx)
1885  {
1886  steep = x1; x1 = y1; y1 = steep; /* swap x1 and y1 */
1887  steep = dx; dx = dy; dy = steep; /* swap dx and dy */
1888  steep = sx; sx = sy; sy = steep; /* swap sx and sy */
1889  steep = 1;
1890  }
1891 
1892  int e = 2 * dy - dx;
1893 
1894  for (int i = 0; i < dx; ++i)
1895  {
1896  if (steep)
1897  plot_pen_pixel(y1,x1);
1898  else
1899  plot_pen_pixel(x1,y1);
1900 
1901  while (e >= 0)
1902  {
1903  y1 += sy;
1904  e -= (dx << 1);
1905  }
1906 
1907  x1 += sx;
1908  e += (dy << 1);
1909  }
1910 
1911  plot_pen_pixel(x2,y2);
1912  }

1914  void horiztonal_line_segment(int x1, int x2, int y)
1915  {
1916  if (x1 > x2)
1917  {
1918  std::swap(x1,x2);
1919  }
1920 
1921  for (int i = 0; i < (x2 - x1); ++i)
1922  {
1923  plot_pen_pixel(x1 + i,y);
1924  }
1925  }

1927  void vertical_line_segment(int y1, int y2, int x)
1928  {
1929  if (y1 > y2)
1930  {
1931  std::swap(y1,y2);
1932  }
1933 
1934  for (int i = 0; i < (y2 - y1); ++i)
1935  {
1936  plot_pen_pixel(x, y1 + i);
1937  }
1938  }

1940  void ellipse(int centerx, int centery, int a, int b)
1941  {
1942  int t1 = a * a;
1943  int t2 = t1 << 1;
1944  int t3 = t2 << 1;
1945  int t4 = b * b;
1946  int t5 = t4 << 1;
1947  int t6 = t5 << 1;
1948  int t7 = a * t5;
1949  int t8 = t7 << 1;
1950  int t9 = 0;
1951 
1952  int d1 = t2 - t7 + (t4 >> 1);
1953  int d2 = (t1 >> 1) - t8 + t5;
1954  int x = a;
1955  int y = 0;
1956 
1957  int negative_tx = centerx - x;
1958  int positive_tx = centerx + x;
1959  int negative_ty = centery - y;
1960  int positive_ty = centery + y;
1961 
1962  while (d2 < 0)
1963  {
1964  plot_pen_pixel(positive_tx,positive_ty);
1965  plot_pen_pixel(positive_tx,negative_ty);
1966  plot_pen_pixel(negative_tx,positive_ty);
1967  plot_pen_pixel(negative_tx,negative_ty);
1968 
1969  ++y;
1970 
1971  t9 = t9 + t3;
1972 
1973  if (d1 < 0)
1974  {
1975  d1 = d1 + t9 + t2;
1976  d2 = d2 + t9;
1977  }
1978  else
1979  {
1980  x--;
1981  t8 = t8 - t6;
1982  d1 = d1 + (t9 + t2 - t8);
1983  d2 = d2 + (t9 + t5 - t8);
1984  negative_tx = centerx - x;
1985  positive_tx = centerx + x;
1986  }
1987 
1988  negative_ty = centery - y;
1989  positive_ty = centery + y;
1990  }
1991 
1992  do
1993  {
1994  plot_pen_pixel(positive_tx,positive_ty);
1995  plot_pen_pixel(positive_tx,negative_ty);
1996  plot_pen_pixel(negative_tx,positive_ty);
1997  plot_pen_pixel(negative_tx,negative_ty);
1998 
1999  x--;
2000  t8 = t8 - t6;
2001 
2002  if (d2 < 0)
2003  {
2004  ++y;
2005  t9 = t9 + t3;
2006  d2 = d2 + (t9 + t5 - t8);
2007  negative_ty = centery - y;
2008  positive_ty = centery + y;
2009  }
2010  else
2011  d2 = d2 + (t5 - t8);
2012 
2013  negative_tx = centerx - x;
2014  positive_tx = centerx + x;
2015  }
2016  while (x >= 0);
2017  }
2018 
2019  void circle(int centerx, int centery, int radius)
2020  {
2021  int x = 0;
2022  int d = (1 - radius) << 1;
2023 
2024  while (radius >= 0)
2025  {
2026  plot_pen_pixel(centerx + x,centery + radius);
2027  plot_pen_pixel(centerx + x,centery - radius);
2028  plot_pen_pixel(centerx - x,centery + radius);
2029  plot_pen_pixel(centerx - x,centery - radius);
2030 
2031  if ((d + radius) > 0)
2032  d -= ((--radius) << 1) - 1;
2033  if (x > d)
2034  d += ((++x) << 1) + 1;
2035  }
2036  }
2037 
2038  void plot_pen_pixel(int x, int y)
2039  {
2040  switch (pen_width_)
2041  {
2042  case 1 : plot_pixel(x,y);
2043  break;
2044 
2045  case 2 : {
2046  plot_pixel(x , y );
2047  plot_pixel(x + 1, y );
2048  plot_pixel(x + 1, y + 1);
2049  plot_pixel(x , y + 1);
2050  }
2051  break;
2052 
2053  case 3 : {
2054  plot_pixel(x , y - 1);
2055  plot_pixel(x - 1, y - 1);
2056  plot_pixel(x + 1, y - 1);
2057 
2058  plot_pixel(x , y );
2059  plot_pixel(x - 1, y );
2060  plot_pixel(x + 1, y );
2061 
2062  plot_pixel(x , y + 1);
2063  plot_pixel(x - 1, y + 1);
2064  plot_pixel(x + 1, y + 1);
2065  }
2066  break;
2067 
2068  default : plot_pixel(x,y);
2069  break;
2070  }
2071  }
2072 
2073  void plot_pixel(int x, int y)
2074  {
2075  image_.set_pixel(x,y,pen_color_red_,pen_color_green_,pen_color_blue_);
2076  }
2077 
2078  void pen_width(const unsigned int& width)
2079  {
2080  if ((width > 0) && (width < 4))
2081  {
2082  pen_width_ = width;
2083  }
2084  }
2085 
2086  void pen_color(const unsigned char& red,
2087  const unsigned char& green,
2088  const unsigned char& blue)
2089  {
2090  pen_color_red_ = red;
2091  pen_color_green_ = green;
2092  pen_color_blue_ = blue;
2093  }
2094 
2095 private:
2096 
2097  image_drawer(const image_drawer& id);
2098  image_drawer& operator =(const image_drawer& id);
2099 
2100  bitmap_image& image_;
2101  unsigned int pen_width_;
2102  unsigned char pen_color_red_;
2103  unsigned char pen_color_green_;
2104  unsigned char pen_color_blue_;
2105 };
